Eagerly we would install you; eagerly we would kindle you.
Eagerly convey the eager forefathers here, to eat the oblation.

English translation:

тАЬYou, Soma, are thoroughly apprehended by our understanding; you lead us along a straight path; by your guidance, Indra, our righteous fathers obtained wealth among the gods.тАЭ

Jamison Brereton

You, Soma, have become conspicuous through our inspired thought. YouтАФlead along the straightest path.
Through your guidance, o drop, our insightful forefathers had their
share in the treasure among the gods.

Jamison Brereton Notes

The multiple possible meanings of the root(s) тИЪcit and the unclear morphological identity of (pr├б) cikitaс╕е make the interpretation of the first p─Бda somewhat difficult. I follow ThiemeтАЩs solution (Plusq.), adopted also by K├╝mmel (176-77), that it is underlyingly a medial injunctive to the perfect stem (that is, an unaugmented pluperfect), patterning with pf. cikit├й, etc. But the underspecification of this posited

*cikita caused it to be re-marked with an active ending (like root presents of the type aduha-t). It should not be a subjunctive, despite its thematic appearance, because of the zero-grade root syllable, and, pace Witzel Got┼Н, it should not be a trans./caus.

reduplicated aorist because of the light reduplicating syllable (expect *c─лkitas) – although I do have to admit that acikitat in VII.80.2 does seem to function like a redupl. aorist. Witzel Got┼Н supply panth─Б╠Бm, from b, as object in a, but this seems unnecessary. On a potential ring made by pr├б cikitaс╕е here and pr├б cikits─Б in the last p─Бda of the hymn (23d), see published introduction. The other question in p─Бda a is whose inspired thought is at issue. I assume that it is ours (that is, the poetsтАЩ), in that the priests and poets create the ritual that makes soma manifest.

Wilson

English translation:

тАЬSoma Pavam─Бna, by you our ancient and wise progenitors performed their religious rites; harming the foes (yourself) unharmed slay the r─Бkс╣гasas and be liberal in enriching us with male offspring and horses.тАЭ

Commentary by S─Бyaс╣Зa: с╣Ъgveda-bh─Бс╣гya

Yourself unharmed: avataс╕е = tair, i.e. ┼Ыatrubhir abhigataс╕е

Jamison Brereton

Because with you, self-purifying Soma, our insightful forefathers performed their (ritual) acts,
open up the barriers, vanquishing but unvanquished; become a
benefactor to us with heroes and with horses.

Jamison Brereton Notes

As Geldner (see n. 11c) and Ober (I.311 with n. 791) point out, the first hemistich depicts the Vala myth, with тАЬforefathersтАЭ (pit├бraс╕е) a reference to the Aс╣Еgirases - made clearer by a similar but more explicit passage in the next hymn, IX.97.39. This mythic episode - the forefathers opening the Vala cave with the help of soma - provides the model for the appeal in c, for Soma to open the paridh├н- (paridh─л╠Бm╠Рr ├бporс╣Зu): paridh├н- is used explicitly of the barriers of the Vala cave in I.52.5. But as Geldner suggests (n. 11c), the poet here is calling on Soma to open up the livestock pens and provide us with the animals therein.

Griffith

For our sage fathers, Soma Pavamana, of old performed, by thee, their sacred duties.
Fighting unvanquished, open the enclosures: enrich us with large gifts of steeds and heroes.

Geldner

Denn mit dir, o Soma, haben unsere weisen V├дter vormals ihre Taten getan, o Pavamana. Ein un├╝berwundener ├Ьberwinder ├╢ffne du die Schranken; sei gegen uns freigebig mit S├╢hnen und Rossen!

Grassmann

Denn unsre alten weisen V├дter thaten durch dich, o heller Soma, ihre Werke, Die Wehren brich unangefochten, siegreich, sei m├дchtig uns durch Helden und durch Rosse.

Elizarenkova

Wilson

English translation:

тАЬSoma, you in conjunction with the fathers do stretch our successively heaven and earth– to you let usdo worship with oblations, may we be lords of wealth.тАЭ

Jamison Brereton

You, Soma, coming to agreement with the forefathers, extend through heaven and earth.
To you, drop, we would do ceremonial honor with an oblation. May we be lords of riches.

Griffith

Associate with the Fathers thou, O Soma, hast spread thyself abroad through earth and heaven.
So with oblation let us serve thee, Indu, and so let us become the lords of riches,

Macdonell

Uniting with the Fathers thou, O Soma, Hast over Heaven and Earth thyself extended. So, Indu, we would serve thee with oblation: Thus we would be the lords of ample riches.

Geldner

Du, Soma, bist mit den V├дtern im Einvernehmen, du reichst so weit wie Himmel und Erde. Dir, o Saft, wollen wir darum mit Opfer aufwarten; wir wollen Herren der Reicht├╝mer sein.

Grassmann

O Soma, du vereinigt mit den V├дtern, hast dich verbreitet ├╝ber Erd’ und Himmel; Dem Indu m├╢chten wir mit Opfer dienen, und m├╢chten sein Besitzer aller Sch├дtze.

Elizarenkova

рдЕрдЧреНрдирд┐рд╖реНрд╡рд╛рддреНрддрд╛рдГ рдЕрдЧреНрдирд┐рдирд╛ рд╕реНрд╡рд╛рджрд┐рддрд╛ рдПрддрдиреНрдирд╛рдордХрд╛рдГ рдкрд┐рддрд░рдГ рдпреВрдпрдореН рдЗрд╣ рдЕрд╕реНрдорд┐рдиреН рдкрд┐рддреГрдХрд░реНрдордгрд┐ рдЖ рдЧрдЪреНрдЫрдд ред рдЖрдЧрддреНрдп рдЪ рд╣реЗ рд╕реБрдкреНрд░рдгреАрддрдпрдГ рдЕрднрд┐рдкреВрдЬрд┐рддрдкреНрд░рдгрдпрдирд╛рдГ рдпреВрдпрдВ рд╕рджрдГрд╕рджрдГ рддрддреНрддрддреНрд╕реНрдерд╛рдирдВ рд╕рджрдд рд╕реАрджрдд ред рддрддреНрд░ рддрддреНрд░ рд╕реНрдерд╛рдиреЗ рдпрдереЗрд╖реНрдЯрдореБрдкрд╡рд┐рд╢рддреЗрддреНрдпрд░реНрдердГред рдЙрдкрд╡рд┐рд╢реНрдп рдЪ рдмрд░реНрд╣рд┐рд╖рд┐ рдЖрд╕рд╛рджрд┐рддрд╛рдирд┐ рдкреНрд░рдпрддрд╛рдирд┐ рд╢реБрдЪреАрдирд┐ рд╣рд╡реАрдВрд╖рд┐ рдЕрддреНрдд рднрдХреНрд╖рдпрдд ред рдЕрде рдЕрдирдиреНрддрд░рдВ рд╕рд░реНрд╡рд╡реАрд░рдВ рд╕рд░реНрд╡реИрд░реНрд╡реАрд░реИрдГ рдкреБрддреНрд░рдкреМрддреНрд░реИрд░реБрдкреЗрддрдВ рд░рдпрд┐рдВ рдзрдирдВ рджрдзрд╛рддрди рдЕрд╕реНрдорднреНрдпрдВ рджрддреНрдд рее

Wilson

English translation:

тАЬAgniс╣гv─Бtta Pitс╣Ыs, come to this solemnity; sit down, directors in the right way, in your appropriateplaces; eat the oblations spread on the grass, and grant us riches and male posterity.тАЭ

Jamison Brereton

Sweetened by Agni, o forefathers, come here. Sit each on his own seat, you of good guidance.
Eat the oblations set forth on the ritual grass. Then provide wealth in hale heroes.

Griffith

Fathers whom Agni’s flames have tasted, come ye nigh: ye kindly leaders, take ye each your proper place.
Eat sacrificial food presented on the grass: grant riches with a multitude of hero sons.

Geldner

Ihr vom Feuer schmackhaft befundenen V├дter, kommet hierher, setzet euch jeder an seinen Platz, ihr guten F├╝hrer! Esset die auf dem Barhis dargereichten Opferspenden und verleihet dann einen Schatz von lauter S├╢hnen!

Grassmann

Ihr einst verzehrt vom Feuer naht, o V├дter, euch, die sch├╢n ihr leitet, setzet euch auf Sitz f├╝r Sitz; Geniesst die dargereichten Speisen auf der Streu und schenkt uns Gut, das alle M├дnner reichlich n├дhrt.

Elizarenkova

English translation:

тАЬPitс╣Ыs, Barhiс╣гads, protect (us who are) in your presence; we have made these oblations for you,accept them; come with your most felicitous protection, and bestow upon us health and happiness; and pardonfrom sin.тАЭ

Commentary by S─Бyaс╣Зa: с╣Ъgveda-bh─Бс╣гya

With your most felicitous protection: avas─Б ┼Ыantamena = satisfied by most excellent food

Jamison Brereton

You forefathers who sit on the ritual grass inclined this way with your aid, we have made these oblations for you. Enjoy!
Come here with your most luck-bringing help. Then provide for us luck and lifetime without flaw.

Griffith

Fathers who sit on sacred grass, come, help us: these offerings have we made for you; accept them.
So come to us with most auspicious favour, and give us health and strength without a trouble.

Elizarenkova

English translation:

тАЬI have brought to my presence the Pitс╣Ыs who are well cognizant (of my worship), the infallibility, andfood of the effused (Soma) with the sacrificial cake.тАЭ

Commentary by S─Бyaс╣Зa: с╣Ъgveda-bh─Бс╣гya

The infallibility…sacrifice: nap─Бtam, vikramaс╣Зam = paths ofthe gods, whence there is no falling and where there is going and coming– both as the consequence of sacrifice(Yajus. 29.56)

English translation:

тАЬMay the Pitс╣Ыs who are entitled to the Soma come, when invoked by us, to the agreeable treasuresconnected with the sacred grass; let them here listen (to our praises), let them speak (their approbation in reply);let them protect us.тАЭ

Commentary by S─Бyaс╣Зa: с╣Ъgveda-bh─Бс╣гya

Entitled to the Soma: somy─Бsaс╕е = anugraha par─Бс╕е, kind or favourable,somasamp─Бdinaс╕е, obtaining the Soma

Jamison Brereton

The forefathers deserving of soma have been summoned here to the dear stores on the ritual grass.
Let them come hither, let them listen (to us) here; let them speak on
(our) behalf, let them help us.1394 X.16

Griffith

May they, the Fathers, worthy of the Soma, invited to their favourite oblations.
Laid on the sacred grass, come nigh and listen: may they be gracious unto us and bless us.

Geldner

Die somaw├╝rdigen V├дter sind jetzt geladen zu den beliebten, auf das Barhis gesetzten Auftischungen. Die sollen herkommen, die sollen hier zuh├╢ren, die sollen uns F├╝rsprecher und gewogen sein!

Grassmann

Geladen sind die Soma-frohen V├дter zu lieben Speisen, welche auf der Streu stehn; Sie m├╢gen kommen und uns hier erh├╢ren und freundlich zu uns reden und uns helfen.

Wilson

English translation:

тАЬLet the lower, the upper, the intermediate Pitс╣Ыs, rise up, accepting the Soma libation; may thoseprogenitors who, unlike wolves, acknowledging our offerings, have come to preserve our lives, protect us uponour invocations.тАЭ

Commentary by S─Бyaс╣Зa: с╣Ъgveda-bh─Бс╣гya

Pitс╣Ыs: three chief classes of the Pitс╣Ыs or manes are enumerated. RV 10.14.6 enumerated aс╣Еgirasas, atharvasand bhс╣Ыgus; in Manu, the three classes are: agni┼Ыv─Бttas, barhiс╣гads and saumy─Бs; Manu’s enumerationoccurs in this s┼лkta; lower, upper and intermediate pitс╣Ыs: the degrees of merit arise first from the steadydischarge of duties enjoined by the Vedas; secondly, by performance of those enjoined by the law books; andfinally, when there has been some deficiency in some of the purificatory rites (saс╣Гsk─Бras);

Udiratam = let themobtain the best oblation; or, urdhvalokam gacchantu, let them go to the upper region (Yajus. 19.49);

Unlikewolves: avс╣Ыk─Бс╕е = not wolves, i.e., not mischievous;

с╣Ъtaj├▒aс╕е = knowing truth; or, grateful for what has beendone in their honour; asum ya ─лyuс╕е = who have gone to life, or breath, asmatpr─Бс╣Зam rakс╣гitum pr─Бptaс╕е; or,identical with air, having assumed the form of the air

Jamison Brereton

Let the nearer ones rise up, up the further, up those in the middleтАФthe forefathers deserving of soma.
Those who have gone to (their next) life avoiding the wolf, knowing the truth, let those forefathers help us at the invocations.

Griffith

MAY they ascend, the lowest, highest, midmost, the Fathers who deserve a share of Soma-
May they who have attained the life of spirits, gentle and righteous, aid us when we call them.

Geldner

Es sollen sich die n├дheren, die ferneren und die mittleren somaw├╝rdigen V├дter aufmachen, die ungef├дhrdet zum Leben eingegangen sind, des Rechten kundig. Diese V├дter sollen uns bei den Anrufungen gewogen sein.

Grassmann

Erheben m├╢gen sich die ersten V├дter, die letzten und die mittelsten, die frommen, Die ohne Leid ins Geisterreich gelangt sind, bei Festen sein uns hold die opferkund’gen.

Elizarenkova

рдпрджреНрд╡рд╛ - рдкреГрдерд┐рд╡реАрд╕рдВрдмрдиреНрдзрд┐рдирд┐ рд▓реЛрдХреЗ рд╕реНрдерд┐рддрд╛рдГ ред рдиреВрдирдорд┐рддрд┐ рдкрд╛рджрдкреВрд░рдгреЗ ред рдпреЗ рд╡рд╛ рд╕реБрд╡реГрдЬрдирд╛рд╕реБ рд╢реЛрднрдирдзрдирд╛рд╕реБ рд╡рд┐рдХреНрд╖реБ рдкреНрд░рдЬрд╛рд╕реБ рдХрд░реНрдорд╢реАрд▓рд╛рд╕реБ рдирд┐рд╖рдгреНрдгрд╛рдГ ред рдпрджреНрд╡рд╛ - рдЙрдкрд░рд╛рд╕рдГ рдЙрдкрд░рдгрд╢реАрд▓рд╛рдГ рдирд┐рд╡реГрддреНрддрд┐рдкреНрд░рдзрд╛рдирд╛рдГ рдкрд╛рд░реНрдерд┐рд╡реЗ рдкреГрдерд┐рд╡реНрдпрд╛рдВ рднрд╡реЗ рд░рдЬрд╕рд┐ рдХрд░реНрдордгрд┐ рдкреБрдгреНрдпрд╛рдкреБрдгреНрдпрд╛рддреНрдордХреЗ рд╡реНрдпрд╛рдорд┐рд╢реНрд░реЗ рдирд┐рд╖рдгреНрдгрд╛рдГ рд╕реБрд╡реГрдЬрдирд╛рд╕реБ рд╢реЛрднрдирдзрдирд╛рд╕реБ рдХрд░реНрдорд╢реЗрд╖рдзрдирд╛рд╕реБ рдзрд╛рд░реНрдорд┐рдХреЗрд╖реБ рдЕрдкрд╛рдкрд╛рд╕реБ рдкреНрд░рдЬрд╛рд╕реБ рдирд┐рд╖рдгреНрдгрд╛рдГ рддреЗрднреНрдпрд╕реНрд╕рд░реНрд╡реЗрднреНрдпреЛ рдирдореЛрд╜рд╕реНрддреНрд╡рд┐рддрд┐ рее

Wilson

English translation:

тАЬLet this our adoration be today addressed to those Pitс╣Ыs our predecessors, to those our successors,who have departed (to the world of the manes); to those who are seated in the terrestrial sphere, to those whoare present among opulent people.тАЭ

Commentary by S─Бyaс╣Зa: с╣Ъgveda-bh─Бс╣гya

Our successors: p┼лrv─Бsaс╕е = elder brother, father, grandfather, and thelike, born before the birth of the worshipper; upar─Бsaс╕е means younger brothers, sons, etc. ; or, those who havegone to svarga; upar─Бsaс╕е, those who have ceased or rested, who have gone to the world of brahm─Б (Yajuс╣г19.68); in the terrestrial sphere: p─Бrthive rajasi = pс╣Ыthiv─лsambandhini rajo guс╣Зak─Бryesmin karmaс╣Зi, at thisritw which is connected with the earth is the effect of (or has for its effect) the quality of rajas (passion, or theactive principle);

Rajas = jyotiс╣г, light– terrestrial light or fire– the phrase no doubt refers to the fire altar (Yajuс╣г19.68)

Jamison Brereton

Let this homage here today be for the forefathersтАФthose who went previously, those who went later,
those who are seated here in the earthly realm, or who are now among the clans of good community.

Griffith

Now let us pay this homage to the Fathers, to those who passed of old and those who followed,
Those who have rested in the earthly region, and those who dwell among the Mighty Races.

Wilson

English translation:

тАЬThus, Agni, our excellent and ancient forefathers, celebrators of holy sacrifice, proceeded to (the region of) pure light, and, reciting prayers and dispersing gloom, they made manifest the purple (kine).тАЭ

Commentary by S─Бyaс╣Зa: с╣Ъgveda-bh─Бс╣гya

Yajus. 19.69; proceeded to the region of pure light: ┼Ыucid ayan d─лdhitim d─лptam sth─Бnam tejas c─Бgacchan: ravi-maс╣Зс╕Нalam, the orb of the sun; the last phrases: may we, dividing the rays of the sun and piercing the earth (with sacrificial posts), also proceed by the path of the gods; or to heaven;

Apavran = ap─Бvс╣Ыс╣Зumaс╕е, with the sense of the potential

Jamison Brereton

Then like our further forefathers of old, panting over the truth, o Agni, those reciting solemn speech (now) will come to the blazing (udder of sacrifice [=Vala]), to visionary power. Splitting (heaven and) earth, they (will) unclose the ruddy (cows [=dawns]).

Jamison Brereton Notes

On с╣Ыt├бm ─Б┼Ыuс╣г─Бn─Б╠Бс╕е see comm. ad IV.1.13.

This vs. has double temporal reference, to the Aс╣Еgirases of long ago using sacred speech to split the Vala cave and release the cows and to the current priests, who imitate the speech of the Aс╣Еgirases in order to release the dawns from darkness.

The failure to realize the double reference to both the opening of Vala and the beginning of the current dawn sacrifice has caused interpretational difficulties. To begin with, ┼Ы├║ci in c has been puzzled over. Oldenberg (SBE) attempted to make it a fem. adj. modifying d─л╠Бdhitim, but in the Noten opts rather for an adverbial neut.

Most other tr. interpr. it as an abstract тАШKlarheitтАЩ vel sim. (Geldner, Renou, Scarlatta [530], sim.

Schmidt [Bс╣Ыhaspati und Indra 43-44]), while Witzel Got┼Н take it as the modifier of с╣Ыt├бm in the preceding p─Бda. I do not know of other exx. of ┼Ы├║ci- in abstract value; I interpr. it rather in conjunction with the phrase ┼Ы├║cy ┼л╠Бdhaс╕е тАж g├бv─Бm тАЬthe gleaming/blazing udder of cowsтАЭ in the preceding hymn (IV.1.19). As noted in the comm. there, I take this as a ref. to the Vala cave. But this тАЬblazing (udder)тАЭ can also refer to the current sacrifice, with the newly kindled fire at its focus. The priests approach this with their sacred speech to set the ritual in motion and achieve d─л╠Бdhitim тАШvisionary powerтАЩ.

I think p─Бda c is appropriate for both the ancient Aс╣Еgirases and the presentday ritualists, and so I would modify the published translation somewhat. The verb ayan is a subjunctive to the root present of тИЪi and therefore primarily applicable to the ritualists and the actions they will now perform. But I also think that itтАЩs possible to interpr. it as a backformed injunctive to the same root present. Since augmented imperfects to stems beginning with a vowel always have lengthened augment (here, well-attested 3rd pl. ─Бyan тАШthey wentтАЩ), it would be possible to form an injunctive by тАЬsubtractingтАЭ the augment a-, producing ayan, rather than the more proper yan (found only in III.4.5). By such an interpr. the Aс╣Еgirases could also be subjects of the verb: they came (inj.) to the gleaming/blazingVala cave (represented by ┼Ы├║ci), and the priests will come (subj.) to the gleaming/blazing place of sacrifice.

The Pp. reads kс╣г─Б╠Бm─Б in d as kс╣г─Б╠Бma, and most interpr. (save for Witzel Got┼Н) follow the Pp. and take this form as a singular, tr. тАЬsplitting the earthтАЭ – as a reference only to the Vala myth (even though it is not the earth that gets split in that myth). But I think we should take the Saс╣Гhit─Б form seriously, as the elliptical dual it appears to be, extracted from the dual dvandva dy─Б╠Бv─Б-kс╣г─Б╠Бm─Б. The phrase тАЬsplitting (heaven and) earthтАЭ would refer to the visual experience of dawn, when the appearance of the dawn light at the horizon seems to split sky from earth, allowing the light to flood in through the resulting slit.

Griffith

As in the days of old our ancient Fathers, speeding the work of holy worship, Agni,
Sought pure light and devotion, singing praises; they cleft the ground and made red Dawns apparent.

And as our first, ancient fathers, O Agni, were aspiring after Rita 1тАФthey attained to pure devotion 2, chanting their litanies. Cleaving the earth they disclosed the red (cows).

English translation:

тАЬAgni J─Бtavedas, who are glorified (by us), having made our oblations fragrant, you have borne themoff, and have presented them to the Pitс╣Ыs; may they partake of them with the Svadh─Б; and do you also, divineAgni, feed upon the offered oblations.тАЭ

Commentary by S─Бyaс╣Зa: с╣Ъgveda-bh─Бс╣гya

Yajus. 19.66: j─Бtavedas = kavyav─Бhana; with the svadh─Б:svadh─Бk─Бreс╣Зa, i.e., with the exclamation, svadh─Б! or, it may mean, along with the svadh─Б or pitс╣Ы-oblationitself

Jamison Brereton

You, Agni J─Бtavedas, reverently invoked, have conveyed the oblations, having made them very fragrant.
You have presented them to the forefathers; they have eaten them at
(the cry of) тАЬsvadh─Б.тАЭ (Now) you, o godтАФeat the oblations set forth.

Griffith

Thou, Agni Jatavedas, when entreated, didst bear the offerings which thou madest fragrant,
And give them to the Fathers who did cat them with Svadha. Eat, thou God, the gifts we bring thee.

Wilson

English translation:

тАЬM─Бtalin prospers with the Kavyas; Yama with the Aс╣Еgirasas; Bс╣Ыhaspati with the с╣Ъkvans; they whomthe gods augment, and they who augment the gods, these rejoice in Sv─Бh─Б, those in the Svadh─Б.тАЭ

Commentary by S─Бyaс╣Зa: с╣Ъgveda-bh─Бс╣гya

M─Бtaliс╣ЕM─Бtal─л is the name of the charioteer of Indra; so M─Бtalin (having M─Бtal─л) is a name of Indra

Jamison Brereton

M─Бtal─л having been strengthened along with the poets, Yama with the Aс╣Еgirases, Br╠еhaspati with the versifiers,
both those whom the gods strengthen and who strengthen the godsтАФ the ones [=gods] become exhilarated on (the cry) тАЬsv─Бh─Б,тАЭ the others [=forefathers] on тАЬsvadh─Б.тАЭ

Griffith

Mitali prospers there with Kavyas, Yama with Angiras’ sons, Brhaspati with Rkvans:
Exalters of the Gods, by Gods exalted, some joy in praise and some in our oblation.

Geldner

Matali mit den Kavya┬┤s, Yama mit den Angiras, Brihaspati von den S├дngern erh├╢ht, welchen die G├╢tter zur Erh├╢hung verholfen haben und welche den G├╢ttern: die einen erg├╢tzen sich unter Svaharuf, die anderen an der G├╢tterspeise.

Grassmann

Dort freut sich Matali mit Kavja’s, Jama mit Angiras, Brihaspati mit Rikvan’s, Gelabt von G├╢ttern sie, von diesen jene, durch Heilsruf jene, und durch Trank die andern.

Elizarenkova

рдмреНрд░рд╣реНрдордореБрдирд┐ - рднрд╛рд╡рд╛рд░реНрдердГ

English translation:

тАЬYama, who are associated with the Aс╣Еgirasa Pitс╣Ыs, sit down at this sacrifice; may the prayers recitedby the priests bring you here; be exhilarated, Sovereign, (Yam), by this oblation.тАЭ

Commentary by S─Бyaс╣Зa: с╣Ъgveda-bh─Бс╣гya

At this sacrifice: prastara = acouch or bed (something strewed)

Jamison Brereton

This strewn grass here, YamaтАФjust sit here on it, in concord with the Aс╣Еgirases, our forefathers.
Let mantras pronounced by poets convey you hither. Become exhilarated on this oblation, o king.

Griffith

Come, seat thee on this bed of grass, O Yama, in company with Angirases and Fathers.
Let texts recited by the sages bring thee O King, let this oblation make thee joyful.

Macdonell

Upon this sacred grass sit down, O Yama, Uniting with the Aс╣Еgiras, our fathers. Let spells recited by the sages bring thee; Do thou, O king, rejoice in this oblation.

Geldner

Setze dich, Yama, darum auf diesen Grasb├╝schel in Eintracht mit den Angiras┬┤, den V├дtern! Die von den Sehern vorgetragenen Dichterworte sollen dich herf├╝hren. Erg├╢tze dich an diesem Opfer, o K├╢nig!

Grassmann

So setz dich, Jama, hin auf diesen Grassitz, vereint den Angiras und unsern V├дtern; Dich fahre her der Liederklang der S├дnger, erg├╢tz dich hier an unserm Trank, o K├╢nig.

Elizarenkova

Wilson

English translation:

тАЬCome here, Yama, with the venerable multiform Aс╣Еgirasas, and be exhilarated; I summon Vivasvat,who is your father, to this sacrifice; be seated on the sacred grass (delight the sacrificer).тАЭ

Jamison Brereton

With the Aс╣Еgirases, deserving of the sacrifice, come hither; Yama, become exhilarated here along with the Vair┼лpasтАФ
I call upon Vivasvant, who is your fatherтАФonce having sat down at this sacrifice, on this ritual grass here.

Griffith

Come, Yama, with the Angirases the Holy, rejoice thee here with children of Virupa.
To sit on sacred grass at this our worship, I call Vivasvan, too, thy Father hither.

Macdonell

Come hither with the Aс╣Еgiras, the holy: Here with Vir┼лpa’s sons, O Yama revel, Vivasvant I invoke, who is thy father, When at this rite upon the straw he’s seated.

Geldner

Komm mit den opferw├╝rdigen Angiras┬┤! O Yama, erg├╢tze dich hier mit den Vairupa┬┤s - ich lade auch den Vivasvat, der dein Vater ist - nachdem du bei diesem Opfer auf dem Barhis Platz genommen hast.

Grassmann

рдЕрдЩреНрдЧрд┐рд░рд╕рдГ рдЕрдЩреНрдЧрд┐рд░реЛрдирд╛рдордХрд╛рдГ рдЕрдерд░реНрд╡рд╛рдгрдГ рдЕрдерд░реНрд╡рдирд╛рдордХрд╛рдГ рднреГрдЧрд╡рдГ рднреГрдЧреБрдирд╛рдордХрд╛рд╢реНрдЪ рдирдГ рдЕрд╕реНрдорд╛рдХрдВ рдкрд┐рддрд░рдГ рдирд╡рдЧреНрд╡рд╛рдГ рдЕрднрд┐рдирд╡рдЧрдордирдпреБрдХреНрддрд╛рдГ ред рд╕рджрд╛ рдиреВрддрдирд╡рддреНрдкреНрд░реАрддрд┐рдЬрдирдХрд╛ рдЗрддреНрдпрд░реНрдердГред рддреЗ рдЪ рд╕реЛрдореНрдпрд╛рд╕рдГ ред рд╕реЛрдордорд░реНрд╣рдиреНрддреАрддрд┐ рд╕реЛрдореНрдпрд╛рдГ ред рдпрдЬреНрдЮрд┐рдпрд╛рдирд╛рдВ рдпрдЬреНрдЮрд╛рд░реНрд╣рд╛рдгрд╛рдВ рддреЗрд╖рд╛рдВ рд╕реБрдорддреМ рдЕрдиреБрдЧреНрд░рд╣рдпреБрдХреНрддрд╛рдпрд╛рдВ рдмреБрджреНрдзреМ рд╡рдпрдВ рд╕реНрдпрд╛рдо рд╕рд░реНрд╡рджрд╛ рддрд┐рд╖реНрдареЗрдо ред рдЕрдкрд┐ рдЪ рд╕реМрдордирд╕реЗ рднрджреНрд░реЗ рд╕реМрдордирд╕рд╕реНрдп рдХрд╛рд░рдгреЗ рдХрд▓реНрдпрд╛рдгреЗ рдлрд▓реЗ рд╕реНрдпрд╛рдо рд╕рд░реНрд╡рджрд╛ рддрд┐рд╖реНрдареЗрдо рее

рднрдЯреНрдЯрднрд╛рд╕реНрдХрд░-рдЯреАрдХрд╛

The a~Ngirasas, the atharvANs, the bhR^igus, are our ancestors who performed the soma pouring, nine month rite;
may we be favored as these venerable ones and be auspiciously protected.

Wilson
